93b1(kha): gyi dbus chen mtha' dbus med// ma bcos gnas su rtogs pas phyin// skal ldan rnal 'byor rtogs pa yis// theg pa'i khyad par ji snyed pa// shes rab chen
93b2(kha): po skad cig la// chos rnams ro gcig bsdus pa'i bdag/ dbang po nus stobs ldan pa la// ji snyed dran rtogs rgyu ba kun// zag med snying po'i bstan pa ste//
93b3(kha): nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// rang byung rtogs pa'i snying po nyid// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i lung // 'phrul tshig rdo rje lu gu brgyud// gsang ba'i rig
93b4(kha): pa'i kha sbyor te// phyi lta nang lta sems su sbyor// rtsa ba'i phun sum tshogs par bshad// ces gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las
93b5(kha): phun sum tshogs pa rtsa ba gcig tu bshad pa'i le'u ste sum cu brgyad pa'o// / de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/ rang snang

93b7(kha): mchog/ mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// rang gsal sku gsung thugs gang zhig/ de nyid gang gis gsal bar bgyi// khyad par rim par ji ltar 'gyur//

94a3(kha): gsung thugs kyi rtsa ba yin// ji snyed snang grangs thams cad kyi// dbyibs dang kha dog che chung dang // ma lus ji ltar gnas pa dang // 'jig rten 'das
94a4(kha): dang ma 'das pa// phyogs dang ris la sogs pa ni// byang chub snying po'i sku ru shar// byang chub sems kyi sku nyid ni// rig pa phyogs ris med pa'i sku//

94a7(kha): chos rnams ni// rang shar gsung gi mtshan nyid do// ji snyed myong tshor shes pa dang // dran rtogs rgyu ba ma lus pa// ma skyes rdo rje a yi ngang // ma lus

95b7(kha): nges bde sdug dang // bya dang mi bya bcas pa yi// so so rang spyod bsam mi khyab// ma lus kun 'dus byang chub sems// zab mo rang byung bsam mi khyab// 'khor

110a1(kha): nyid/ nam mkha'i mtha' ltar dpag med pa'o// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las ye shes ma
110a2(kha): lus pa'i le'u ste zhe bdun pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/ 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum rgyal
110a3(kha): ba thams cad kyi// mkhyen pa'i ye shes gsal ba'i thugs// zhing khams dus gsum thams cad gzigs// mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// ma 'ongs dus na lung
110a4(kha): bstan pa// bcos ma gnas pa'i dus ni gang // snyigs ma'i dus zhes ji ltar lags// rmad byung gsang ba'i theg pa 'di// dar dang nub par ji ltar 'gyur// ma
110a5(kha): bcos rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas// dus la bzang ngan rtog mi rtog/ 'dus pa'i tshogs la gsal bar gsungs// zhes zhus so/ 6/ de nas rgyal ba kun gyi gsang
110a6(kha): ba'i bdag po des 'di skad ces gsungs so// dus gsum rgyal ba'i dgongs pa dang // ma bcos rang byung snying po dang // rnal 'byor rtogs pa'i rig pa la// dus gsu/
110a7(kha): khyad par mi dmigs kyang // zhen rtogs dbang gis gsum du snang // ma 'ongs dus na lung bstan pa// dus ni rnam pa lnga ru bstan// dpag med bstan pa'i snying po nyid//
110b1(kha): brgyud pa'i sgo nas bstan pa'i phyir// lha dang mi yi sgron ma yis// dpag tu med pa ston par 'gyur// tshad ma mngon du snang ba'i dus// de nas 'dul thabs sna
110b2(kha): tshogs kyang // ma lus mi rtag bstan pa'i phyir// rdo rje lta bu'i sku bshigs nas// mya ngan 'das par gang bstan nas// bstan pa rig par gang gnas pa//
110b3(kha): mngon rtogs dus ni 'byung bar 'gyur// des na dman pas mi rtogs shing // shes bya'i thabs kyis 'gags pa la// tshig dang yi ger kun snang ste// sgron ma
110b4(kha): 'di yis byed par 'gyur// 'di la brtan te gang gnas pa// tshig dang yi ger gnas pa'i dus// de dag don la grar brtags pas// rang rang dbang po khyad par
110b5(kha): gyis phyi nang chos dang rig pa las// spangs dang sbyangs dang dgag byas nas// rtogs nas zhen pa'i lam la gnas// zhi gnas lhag mthong gsal ba'i sems// goms
110b6(kha): pa zad pa zil gnon grub// sper ba'i stobs dang rkyen gyis snang // dgra bcom rkyen rtogs pha rol phyin// rang sa'i 'bras bu nges thob pa// 'di ltar nges par 'byung ba dang //
110b7(kha): log pa'i rgol bas bsgrub pa dang // byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa yis// slar yang snang bar byed par 'gyur// de nas dka' thub ting 'dzin gyis// myur du grub pa 'dod pa'i phyir/
111a1(kha): bya ba dang ni gnyis ka dang // rnal 'byor rgyud du rnam 'phrul nas// de dag sgo nas gang spyad pas// sngags dang phyag rgya ting 'dzin gyis// rnam grong
111a2(kha): sa la 'gro bar 'gyur// de nas zhen pa'i gang zag dag/ mthun par 'dus par gyur dbang gis// dka' thub sdom pa mi spyod cing // 'dod pa lnga la gang zhen pa// brtu la zhugs don
111a3(kha): la spyod pa'i phyir// gsang chen yang gsang theg pa nyid// 'jam gling dbus su dar gyur nas// rig 'dzin sa la 'gro bar 'gyur// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i theg pa yis// lha mi rig 'dzin
111a4(kha): sa la bkod// dang po lha gnas gsum nyid du// de nas 'dzam gling dbus su ste// dgongs pa rim par brgyud nas ni/ skal ldan rnams la snang bar 'gyur// yid bzhin lha yi
111a5(kha): khang pa dang // snying po byang chub rdo rje gdan// kha che'i yul dang o D+yan du// rim par brgyud cing grags par 'gyur// de dag bsgrubs pa'i sgo nas ni// 'bras bu mngon du thob par 'gyur//
111a6(kha): de nas kun tu grags pa yis// mkhas pa mang po 'byung ba dang // grub pa'i mtha' la rtsod par 'gyur// rgyal khams rnam pa bco brgyad kyi// snang ba'i sgron ma byed par 'gyur//
111a7(kha): de nas mtha' 'khob yul du rgyas// skal ldan sa la 'gro bar 'gyur// skal med gsang ba'i dam sri dag/ ngan 'gro gnas su 'khyams par 'gyur// mkhas pas byin rlabs
111b1(kha): bstan pa'i chos// mi nub brtan cing byin rlabs ldan// kun tu grags shing snang bar 'gyur// de nas gsang ba'i theg pa ni// gsang zhing 'ga' la snang ba dang // snying rje med par
111b2(kha): gsod pa dang // bya ba ma yin spyod par 'byung // de nas mos pa tha dad pas// rang rang bzhin pa'i grub mtha' yis// dam pa'i don la skur pa dang // chos la byin rlabs
111b3(kha): chung ba ni// bslad pas log chos rgyas par 'gyur// thun mong theg pa kun 'dus pas// gsang ba'i don la skur par 'gyur// de nas de yi rnam smin gyis// dus
111b4(kha): min 'chi dang bar chad mang // nad dang mu ge 'khrug pa dang // sdug bsngal rnam pa mang po dag/ rgyal khams yongs su 'byung 'gyur te// 'di ni bsgrub pa'i dus su
111b5(kha): bstan// skal ldan ma btsal grol ba dang // 'dod lnga ma spangs rol pa dang // dus kyi snyigs ma'i 'gro ba rnams// nyon mongs zhen pa'i dbang gyur dang // mos chung
111b6(kha): rtsol bzhan mod kyang // grub mtha' ma lus shes 'dod la// ma bcos rdzogs pa chen po nyid// snyigs ma'i dus dang 'brel dus su// dam pa'i theg pa snang bar 'gyur/
111b7(kha): de yang thugs rje'i byin rlabs kyis// lha gnas dag pa'i pho brang gnas// ma spangs rol pa'i theg pa 'di// lha gnas gsum du grags par 'gyur// de nas thugs rje'i
112a1(kha): byin rlabs kyis// dpal ldan o D+yan gling phran de// sems brgyud rig pa'i thor cog can// 'da' shod ko sha gling phug tu// sprul pa'i dbang phyug rdo
112a2(kha): rje'i lus// dam pa'i rgyal po gsang bdag gis// yang sprul thugs kyi rgyal sras la// rang byung rig pa'i sgo phye nas// spyi blugs tshangs pa'i dbang bskur nas//
112a3(kha): rna brgyud lung 'dri ston par 'gyur// de nas yang sbrul thugs sras kyis// skal ldan 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs la// 'dzam gling dbus su ston par 'gyur//
112a4(kha): kun tu 'phel zhing rgyas pa yis// skal ldan dam par nges pa rnams// sangs rgyas sa la 'gro bar 'gyur// skal med rgyun ni rnam gsum gyis// 'dzam gling
112a5(kha): dbus su sbed par 'gyur// de nas thugs rje'i byin rlabs dang // smon lam dad pas 'phangs nas ni// mtha' 'kho ba yul du snang bar 'gyur// skal ldan rigs
112a6(kha): brgyud 'dzin pa rnams// ma bcos rig pa'i don rtogs nas// skad cig tsam gyis grol bar 'gyur// rna brgyud gsang ba'i 'phrul tshig 'di// gsang ba'i rigs can
112a7(kha): 'ga' zhig la// phyin ci log dang dman pa la// mngon du snang bar mi 'gyur ro// de dag gsang ba'i theg pa 'di// rna brgyud gdams pa nub pa dang // lha spyod log pa'i
112b1(kha): gdeng ldan dang // mtshan ma sgra la zhen pa dang // skal bar ldan dang mi ldan pa'i// 'dus pa mang po bstan pa dang // bla ma rang rtog zhan pa yis// nga nyams zhen pas
112b2(kha): bshad pa dang // rnam par dkar ba'i lam bor nas// nyon mongs zhen pa'i las byed dang // thun mong theg pa la smad pas// nyon mongs zhen pas rtsod pa'i mthus// bstan
112b3(kha): pa'i snying po nub par 'gyur// de nas 'dzam gling dbus su dang // skal ldan 'brel pa'ang 'byung bar 'gyur// de nas lho phyogs rgyud du rgyas// nub kyi phyogs su'ang rgyas par
112b4(kha): 'gyur// byang gi phyogs dang shar phyogs su// ma bcos rdzogs pa'i theg pa 'dis// snang ba'i sgron ma byed par 'gyur// der yang skal ldan dam pa rnams// rnam
112b5(kha): grol sa la 'gro bar 'gyur// rna brgyud gter lam chad pa dang // lha spyod log pa'i nga rgyal can// mtshan ma tshig la zhen pa rnams// rdo rje'i khab tu ltung bar 'gyur//
112b6(kha): rang byung byang chub snying po 'di// ma lus snying la gnas pa ste// dus gsum 'gyur ba med pa'i sems// ma bcos sems la 'gyur ba med// de bzhin lung bstan ldan pa yis/
112b7(kha): skal ldan rgyal sras slob ma la// thabs kyis ma bcos don bstan nas// 'khor ba rang grol don rtogs na// dus la 'gyur ba yod ma yin// snga phyi med pa'i da lta nyid//
113a1(kha): ma bcos rtogs pas pha rol phyin// tha ma'i dus na 'byung bar 'gyur// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ lung
113a2(kha): bshad pa'i le'u ste zhe brgyad pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa de la/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum
113a3(kha): rgyal ba thams cad kyi// bstan pa kun gyi rang bzhin khyod// ma lus kun gyi 'byung gnas gter// mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// rang byung thugs su gcig ce na/
113a4(kha): glong dgur dbye ba ji ltar lags// glong zhes ci phyir bya ba lags// gang gi skabs su ji ltar 'char// de dag dgos pa ji lta bu// mgon po khyed kyis bdag la gsungs/
113a5(kha): zhes gsol to// de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes/ 'dus pa'i tshogs la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// ji snyed chos rnams thams cad kun// ci ste tha dad yongs
113a6(kha): kyis med// rang byung rdzogs pa'i theg pa la// ma 'dus pa yi chos mi gnas// rang bzhin snang ba'i chos rnams dang // phyi nang dran rig thams cad dang // bstan pa'i bye brag
113a7(kha): ma lus pa// ji snyed khyad par bstan pa kun// rgya mtsho dang ni rlabs bzhin te// rig pa rang snang ma yin pa// gzhan pa nyid ni yod ma yin// rang byung theg pa'i snying po
113b1(kha): 'di// bstan pa kun gyi bdag nyid pas// rang byung bstan pa kun gyi bdag/ theg pa kun gyi rtsa ba yin// ma bcos snying po rdzogs pa la// tha dad rnam pa mi snang bas//
113b2(kha): rnam par dbye ba'i chos med kyang // rol pa'i snying po dgu ru shar// lta ba phyogs ris med pa'i glong // spyod pa blang dor med par spyod// mtha' dbus med pa'i snying
113b3(kha): po len// rang byung thabs kyis rtogs pa'i dbang // rang byung don la 'das pa med// bya btsal kun bral 'phrin las rdzogs// ma lus dran pasam ting 'dzin/
113b4(kha): glong // ye shes ma bsgribs phyogs ris med// 'bras bu lhun rdzogs bya ba tsal med// rol pa'i bye brag dgur shar yang // byang chub sems la dbye ba med// ji ltar
113b5(kha): snang ba'i chos rnams kun// rang byung rdzogs pa'i ngo bo ste// phyi nang spyod yul dran rtog dang // bde sdug mtho dman ma lus kun// rgyu rkyen ngo bo tha dad med// chu yis
113b6(kha): 'khor lo bskor ba ltar// chu rlabs ri mo cir yang snang // ngo bo gcig tu gnas pa ltar// ji ltar snang grags dran rtog kun// rang byung stong pa'i klong du brda la// ma lus
113b7(kha): byang chub lung du bsdus// rang bzhin gnas dang rtogs pa dang // mthar phyin spyod yul thams cad la// phyogs ris med dang sel med pas// de phyir 'di la glong zhes brjod//
114a1(kha): gzhan du lta bas mi gnas te// tha dad pa dang dgag sgrub dang // gnyis 'dzin rgyu 'bras la sogs pa// phyogs ris sel dang ldan

114a3(kha): byung theg pa'i snying po nyid// dngos dbang gcig las mi gnas kyang // gang zag blo yi bye brag gis// gzhi lam 'bras bur rnam par snang // rang bzhin gnas po'i glong dgu
114a4(kha): dang // ma bcos rtogs pa'i glong dgu dang // thugs rje rol pa'i glong dgu nyid// skabs kyis khyad par so sor snang // ma bcos rol pa rang snang dang // zhen rtags rtog

114a6(kha): gang zag rnams// sbrel ma g.yang du 'brel ba bzhin// bla ma ngan pa'i rjes 'brangs nas// rdo rje'i khab tu ltung gyur nas/ byang chub sems kyi rigs dang bral// ma bcos
114a7(kha): rdzogs pa'i ngo bo nyid// brda tshig zhen brjod kun bral yang // mtshan ma brda tshig zhen pa rnams/ brjod pas don la dgod pa dang // theg pa kun gyi don rnams ni// 'di la
114b1(kha): rdzogs par bstan pa dang // ma 'dres khyab par bstan pa'i phyir// glong dgu'i khyad par bstan pa yin// de dag gang ltar snang gyur kyang // rang byung snying po de shar phyir//
114b2(kha): rgya mtsho chu bo 'du 'phro ltar// ma lus sems su 'dus pa yin// don gcig ma lus kun rdzogs pas/ grong dgu thugs kyi yang snying 'di// rdo rje 'phrul gyi tshig gi/
114b3(kha): bstan// ma bcos rig pa nyams kyis go// bstan pa'i bye brag ji snyed pa// snying po don du kun 'dus pas// dngos don rtogs pa'i skad cig la// bstan pa ma lus
114b4(kha): dus gcig rtogs// snying po ro dang rnam pa ltar// gang ltar snang yang gcig tu myong // tha dad med de ngo bo gcig/ rang bzhin nam mkha'i mtha' ltar khyab// thugs

115a1(kha): gcig/ mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// klong dgu'i bstan pa ji snyed pa// gnas pa'i ngo bo ji ltar gcig/ rtogs pa'i thabs ni ji ltar gcig

117b1(kha): can// gnyis pa dran snang glo bur ba// gsum pa ma bcos nyid du gsal// dang por mi mkhas shes pa ste// gnyis pa mkhas pa'i 'du shes yin// gsum pa ma bcos nyid
117b2(kha): du bstan// dang por dge ba dang du thang // gnyis pa gnyis ka mi len te// gsum pa dge sdig gnyis ka spyod// dang por rtse gcig dgongs pa ste// gnyis pa rdzogs pa'i dngon
117b3(kha): pa yin// gsum pa phyogs ris med pa bstan// ma lus dran rtogs ting 'dzin mchog/ snang ba ma lus rig pa'i nyams// ma bgrod rig pa glong gi sa// dus gcig sangs rgyas
117b4(kha): sa la bkod// ma btsal lhun gyis grub pa nyid// rgyu rkyen bcol pa las 'das pa// rang byang 'od dang rin chen ltar// gzhan las byung dang bsgrubs pa dang // btsal dang bgrod pa'i
117b5(kha): 'bras bu min// rgya mtsho chu dang rba rlabs ltar// sna tshogs snang yang gzhan byung min// rang byung lhun rdzogs 'bras bu la// bdag gzhan don kun rdzogs par gnas//
117b6(kha): ngo bo gcig las ma g.yos kyang // rol pa gzhan don 'bum phrag yas// gang ltar mthun pa'i bsam pa ltar// mdzad pa'i byin rlapas 'od ltar 'phro// ma bcos rdzogs chen
117b7(kha): bstan pa 'di// rna brgyud tshad ma'i don bral zhing // ma bcos don gyi gdeng med na// lung dang sgra dang yid spyod kyis// rgya mtsho 'dzings kyi pha bong ltar// rang snang rtogs pa'i nyams
118a1(kha): med par// gzhan don mdzad pa'i skyes bu des// pha rol ji ltar thar par 'gyur// gnyis ka sbrel ma ga yang 'gril ltar// 'khor ba'i mtha' mar lhung
118a2(kha): gyur nas// re dogs gnas las thar pa med// ces gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ don rnam grangs kyis gtan la phab pa'i le'u steng
118a3(kha): gcig pa'o// // de nas sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/ 'dus pa chen po rig pa rang snang gi 'khor tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum
118a4(kha): rgyal ba thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi dgongs pa che// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// rtsa ba'i snying po las gsungs pa// man ngag dgu rum sbas pa'i gte
118a5(kha): thabs chen gang gis gsal bar bgyi// legs par bdag la bshad du gsol// zhes gsol to// 6/ de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i bdag po
118a6(kha): lag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsungs so// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i gter// rig pa'i 'khor lo yu ba can// rtogs pa ye shes 'khor lo'i mdzod// don gyi snying po gsung
118a7(kha): gi bcud// kun brjod ye shes 'khor lo can// rang bzhin brtags dang bltos pa yi// ma rig mun pas bsgribs pa rnams// gsang ba'i rgyud 'di la brtan nas// da lha nyid du
118b1(kha): dngas par byed// bskal pa stong phrag grangs med par// thabs kyi rtsol ba'i rnam grangs kyis// ji ltar btsal yang mi rnyed de// rang byung snying po rtogs par dka'// e ma'o/
118b2(kha): rab tu rtogs par dka'// a ma'o rang bzhin rnyog pa med// e ma'o ma bcos bde chen po// e ma'o thig le rang byung sems// rdo rje snying po rmad byung ba// nam mkha'i
118b3(kha): mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// man ngag mngon du phyung ba ni// gang du rtsa ba snying po'i phyir// dang po dag ni bstan pa yin// de nyid rgyas par ston pa'i phyir// bcu pa gsal
118b4(kha): par bkod pa yin// de dag tshogs pa'i dgos pa yang // byin rlabs ting 'dzin rig pa yis// rig pa rang 'char bstan mdzad pas// gnyis pa nyid ni bshad pa yin// brgyud
118b5(kha): ba'i gsang nyid bstan pa'i phyir// bzhi pa de ltar bkod pa yin// de dag skal ldan la bstan phyir// nyi shu drug pa bkod pa yin// 'di dag gzhi nyid bstan pa yin// skal
118b6(kha): ldan rigs can rnal 'byor pa// gsang ba'i don la gang gnas pa// legs nyes 'bras bu lung bstan phyir// nyi shu pa nyid bstan pa yin// de nyid dkyil 'khor 'jug
118b7(kha): pa'i phyir// bcu gsum pa nyid bstan pa yin// dam tshig chen po dbog pa'i phyir// bco lnga pa nyid bstan pa yin// de dag nyid la dbang bskur zhing // bcu bzhi pa nyid/
119a1(kha): bstan pa yin// skal ldan dbang tho ba gang zag gis// rna brgyud gdams pa thob dgos pas// bdun pa legs par bkod pa ste// lam gyi
119a2(kha): ngo bo bstan pa yin// bdag don rtogs pa mthar phyin kyang // rdzogs pa tshig gi yan lag gis// bshad bya mdzod dgu'i bstan pa dag/ gang zag de la bstan pa'i phyir//
119a3(kha): lnga pa dag ni bshad pa yin// sems nyid mdzod dgu gter gyi bdag/ glong dgur phye ste bstan pa'i phyir// nyi shu gcig pa bkod pa yin// glong dgu'i bam po nyi khri yi// brjod/
119a4(kha): pa'i lde mig bstan pa'i phyir// gsum pa nyid ni bkod pa yin// de dag nges pa'i gas la rtogs pas// drug pa nyid ni bkod pa yin// gdams ngag med pa'i gang zag la//
119a5(kha): gang gis gang la bsgribs pa'i phyir// dgu pa lags par bkod pa yin// de nyid ma bcos bstan rtogs pas// brgyad pa legs par bstan pa yin// de nyid dbang po'i khyad par/
119a6(kha): gyis// ji ltar 'tsham par bstan pa'i phyir/ nyi shu lnga pa bstan pa yin// de yis yid ches nges pa'i phyir// nyi shu gsum pa bstan pa yin// nges pa rnyed pas glong dgu pa'o//
119a7(kha): rig pa gcig tu rtogs pa'i phyir// nyi shu gnyis pa bstan pa yin// rig pa skye med nyams myong bas// bcu gcig pa nyid bstan pa yin// de nyid bar chad med bsgom pa// bcu
119b1(kha): drug pa nyid gsal bar bstan// gdang du gyur pa'i rnal 'byor pas// sgo gsum spod pa bstan pa'i phyir// bcu gnyis pa nyid bstan pa yin// lha sprod ting 'dzin 'bral goms
119b2(kha): pas/ bya med 'phrin las lhun grub pas// bcu bdun pa nyid bstan pa yin// de ltar rtogs goms rnal 'byor la// sa dang lam la rim med pas// bco brgyad pa nyid
119b3(kha): bstan pa yin// 'di dag yan lag bshad pa yin// da ltar sa lam mthar phyin pas// ya shes lnga rdzogs lhun rdzogs pas// bcu dgu pa nyid bstan pa yin//
119b4(kha): de nyid lhun grub 'bras bu brjod// de ltar rdzogs pa chen po nyid// mtshan gyi don nyid shes bya'i phyir// nyi shu bzhi pa gsal bar bstan// de dag mi nub bstan bya'i phyir//
119b5(kha): nyi shu bdun pa bstan pa yin// rang byung rdzogs pa'i bdud rtsi 'di// rna brgyud 'phrul tshig mi ldan par// rang brtags log pa'i 'du shes kyis// yid spyod rdzogs su
119b6(kha): gang 'jug pa// bla ma slob mar bcas pa rnams// bdud rtsi dug tu gyur pa ltar// lha spyod log pa'i nga rgyal gyis// rdo rje'i khab tu ltung gyur nas// byang chub sems
119b7(kha): kyi rigs dang bral// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ rdo rje snying po'i rgyud man ngag gis gtan la phab pa'i le'u steng gnyis
120a1(kha): pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu 'di skad
120a2(kha): ces gsol to// dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyi// snying po rang byung rgyal po la// skye shi ri dogs mi gnas kyang // thugs rje'i mnga' bdag khyod kyis ni// 'chi bdag ya
120a3(kha): shes la bzlas te// 'gro bar re dogs gcod par mdzod// ces zhus so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i bdag po des 'di skad ces bka'
120a4(kha): stsal to// rang byung rig pa'i rgyal po nyid// ma lus kun gyi rang bzhin yang // de nyid kun bzang rig pa ste// thog ma tha ma dngos med pas// de nyid bde ba chen po la//
120a5(kha): dran rtog pade sdug tsor snang yang // ma bcos bdud rtsi'i thig ler brtag/ rang byung bdud rtsi'i pho brang nas// gsang ba'i thig le 'du zhing 'phro// rtsa ba ma skyes a las byung //
120a6(kha): rtse mo phyogs med nam mkha'i glong // ngo bo thig le mi g.yo ba// brtags pas stong pa'i ngang du thim// gnas pa dang ni rgyu ba dang // thim par rang byung bde chen gsal// ma lus
120a7(kha): bdud rtsi thig le yis// 'chi ba'i re dogs gcad pa yin// bdud rtsi rgyu ba'i rig pa nyid// gang la brten pa'i ye shes te// phyi nang phyogs ris kha dog dbyibs// bar ma'i rig pa
120b1(kha): brtags pa las// nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor mngon du snang // dang po'i dkyil 'khor phyogs med la// gsang ba'i dbang pos bltas pa ltar// dang por mig dang phrad par bya//
120b2(kha): de nas mthong ba'i don la brtag/ rig pa gdeng gi don thob nas// ma lus kun kyang de bzhin te// phyogs med nam mkha'i rang bzhin la// skyes bus ral gri ba tab pa'am//
120b3(kha): dad pa'i rang bzhin 'bigs pa ltar// blan po rtog pas bcings 'gyur gyi// de nyid mthong ba'i rna la 'byor la// 'pho ba'i re dogs gcad pa yin// gang du de dag brtan gyur na//
120b4(kha): rig pa rgyu ba gnyis med pa// smig rgyu rlung dang 'dres pa ltar// de nyid rig pa'i stobs kyis bsgom// de ltar gsal brtan 'jigs bral na// snga phyi skye gnas 'jigs pa med//
120b5(kha): nam mkha' bsgribs med dngas pa la// gsal ba 'char nub med pa ltar// rang bzhin ma skyes phyogs med la// rig pa 'char nub med par brda la// nam zhig slu bar 'dod
120b6(kha): pa na/ rgyu ba rig pa'i thig le nyid// gnas pa a yi dang la bstim// rlung sems nam mkha'i nyams myong gis// bsdus te nam mkha'i glong la tha mi// dang po rgyu ba'i thig le
120b7(kha): ste// gnyis pa rig pa'i thig le ste// gsum pa gnyis med thig le nyid// ma 'phos bar du nges par bya// gang du dman pa'i rnal 'byor la// 'chi bdag dbang po bzlog
121a1(kha): ba'i phyir// bsam gtan gsum gyi rnal 'byor gyi// 'chi ba'i re dogs rnam par gcad// thig le bsdu ba'i ngo bo ni// ji snyed bya ba'i spyod pa ni//
121a2(kha): bdag nyid spyi yi tshul du sdud// de nyid gnas pa 'byung bzhi rlung // 'di dag dus ni gsum yin la// mngon du nges shes mi skye la// bla mas byin gyis ma brlabs na//
121a3(kha): thug phrad lam la rmongs pa dang // 'chi med bdud rtsi don mi rtogs// dus gsum rig pas nges mthong la// rkyen dang ldan pa'i rnal 'byor pas// bar chud ma lus
121a4(kha): bsal byas te// snyan pa'i rol mor bcas pa yis// don dang ldan pa'i sgra gsum gyis// thun tshad nyams dang mnyam sbyar nas// dran dal gsum gyi sgra yis bstan//
121a5(kha): tha ma nyin zhag bdun gyis te// re dogs chad pa nyams myong gis// par mi srid pa'i chos med par// skye ba len pa'i sdug bsngal bral// 'khor ba'i re dogs rnam par

121b1(kha): rgyal ba thams cad kyi// rig pa gsung gi 'khor lo bdag/ brgyud pa gsum gyi gsang ba 'chang // mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// ma lus sems su rang gnas kyang /

121b5(kha): sum nyid// zag pa med pa'i dang sa ma ste// ma lus snying por gcig pa yin// gang du log stobs drag po yis// med las dngos por rags par snang // gang du mthong ba'i
121b6(kha): stobs log pas// rang byung snying po'i 'od la bsgribs// thabs dang bral ba'i rnal 'byor pas// ji ltar bltas kyang don mi mthong // 'phrul tshig brda yis gtan la dbab//
121b7(kha): gsang ba'i don gyi rtogs pas lta// ma bcos yin par bzhag pas bsgom// re dogs med pa'i tshul gyis spyad// stong nyid nam mkha'i rdo rje la// rig pas ma bcos bltas
122a1(kha): pa'i tshe// ma lus nam mkha' chen po nyid// de nyid dngos por snang ba mthong // ma bcos snang ba'i rang bzhin la// rtse gcig dran pas bltas
122a2(kha): pa'i tshe// gang bltas stong nyid rang bzhin te// de dag ji bzhin yin par mthong // snang srid ji snyed ma lus pa// sems nyid thig le'i rang bzhin la// rtogs par 'dod

122a7(kha): rna ba rgyud tshig gsum man ngag gis// tshig dang bral ba mngon du bstan// srog gi thig le rgyu ba yis// rgyu ba med pa'i don du bstan// snang srid mtshan ma'i dngos po yis//
122b1(kha): mtshan med rig pa mngon du bstan// de ltar rig pa'i nyams myong yang // dus gsum nyid kyis shes pa yin// rna brgyud lung gi bdud rtsi yis// ma lus sems su mngon rtogs te// /

122b4(kha): bsgoms sems la yengs pa med// 'phra med rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor la// dus gsum gcig tu brtag pa'am// 'phen pa dang pos mtshams sbyar te// chu bo lta bur ma

123b1(kha): po phyag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// dgongs pa'i rig pa skye ba med// gdod nas rang byung snying po ste// mi phyed rdo rje zhes su bshad/

124b4(kha): bgrod pa'am// rgya mtsho'i snying por gnas pa ltar// sna tshogs zhen pa rang log nas// rig pa'i nyams ni gcig tu gsal// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha'
124b5(kha): dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ rdo rje snying po gtan la phab pa'i le'u ste lnga bcu nga lnga pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/
124b6(kha): 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyis// ye shes rang bzhin khyod yin pas// sangs rgyas kun gyis mdzad par shar// rgyud
124b7(kha): kun 'dus pa'i rtsa ba zhes// rgyal pa rnams kyis gsungs pa'i don// mgon pos bdag cag rnams la gsungs// zhes gsol to// de nas sems dpa' rdo rje dam pas
125a1(kha): 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// rang byung thig le mtshon pa'i thabs// bka' rgyud ma lus thams
125a2(kha): cad kyi/ dam pa'i snying po dri ma med// e ma'o ya shes mchog gi don// e ma'o shin tu rtogs par dka'// e ma'o rgyal ba kun gyi lam// e ma'o mchog tu
125a3(kha): mya ngan 'das// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ye shes snying po dri ma med// rdo rje nam mkha'i dkyil lta bu// dam pa rnams kyis dgongs pa nyid// rdo rje sems

125a5(kha): cad kun// rang thig le'i ngang du bsdu// de nyid phyogs med rang snang bas// sangs rgyas sems can re dogs med// sna tshogs sku gsung thugs su bsdus// de
125a6(kha): nyid rig pa skye med de// rang byung snying po glong thob pas// phyogs 'dzin rnam rtog zil gyis mnan// ji snyed phung po lnga bdag nyid// de nyid gzung 'dzin bdag nyid
125a7(kha): do// dag dang ma dag gcig tu 'dres// bsgom du med pa'i thig ler gsal// mi dmigs yul med thig le nyid// blo rgur 'das pa'i don rtogs nas// yod med
125b1(kha): re dogs chad pa'i lam// phyogs med rang byung kun la 'jug/ ma rtogs 'khor ba'i ru ba ni// rang sems tsa t+ta'i dkyi la 'khor lnga// pad+ma skyon pra la yon ta na wA ra// ma lus
125b2(kha): rmad byung sangs rgyas sa// 'khor 'das ma lus kun gyi rtsa// rang sems ma bcos snying po ste// brtags pas nam mkha' las 'das pa// mtshon cing brtag
125b3(kha): pa'i yul las 'das// rtsu ba med pa'i rig pa nyid// chos rnams kun gyi rtse mo ste// thabs kyis rtogs na byung rgyal nyid// ma lus re dogs bcad pa yin//
125b4(kha): ma lus bdag nyid yin rtogs nas// bdag nyid rtogs pas pha rol phyin// bde bas bde rtogs bde chen rtogs// dam tshig bde rtogs bde ba'i mchog/ srog ni nam
125b5(kha): mkha'i rdo rje ste// 'khor lo bskor ba ma lus gcod// phyi nang snod bcud thams cad kun// mnyam pa chen po'i ngang du bskor// ma lus chos rnams thams cad kyi//
125b6(kha): ngo bo sems su gcig pas na// gsang ba'i thabs chen gcig bstan pas// ma lus kun rtogs rgyal po'o// ma bcos rig pa'i thig le la// bde ba chen po'i thig le
125b7(kha): brtag/ bcos pa med pa'i thig le bde// ji snyed snga phyi chos rnams ni// yul dang shes pa gnyis 'dus te// de nyid ma bcos thig ler 'dus// de nyid rtogs pas
126a1(kha): ro gcig go// ma lus bdag nyid kun rdzogs pas// dag dang ma ngag tshig mtha' 'das// bdag nyid chu ltar gzhan med pas// ma bcos
126a2(kha): rnal du gnas pa nyid// ji snyed tha snyad ma lus pa'i// rig pa kun kya tha snyad spyad// re dog sa 'jigs pa kun bral ba// ma lus kun gyi rtogs bya nyid// ma bcos
126a3(kha): rig pa'i don nyid ni// rna ba rgyud 'phrul gyis rim par bstan// rdo rje gser gyi zhen bkrol nas// tha ma ma bcos ngo bor bstan// khams gsum yid bzhin nor bu
126a4(kha): ste/ stong la yon tan kun 'byung ba// nam mkha'i nor bus dbang bskur nas// rgyal ba kun gyi dbang po yin// ma lus rdzogs pa'i thig le ste// snying po'i dam
126a5(kha): las ma 'das na// dmangs kyi chad pas mi 'jigs ltar// mtshan ma'i skyon gyis mi 'jigs so// ma lus kun byed byang chub sems// rgya mtsho nyi ltar 'jigs
126a6(kha): med pas// re dogs spangs pa'i spyod pa nyid// 'chi med bdud rtsi rgyal po ste// 'di ni rgyal ba thams cad kyi// rgyud do cog gi rtsa ba ste// rdo rje 'dus pa'i snying po
126a7(kha): yin// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ rgyal ba kun gyi dgongs pa'i rtsa ba 'dus pa'i lung gi le'u steng drug pa'o//
126b1(kha): / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gsang ba'i bdag po chen po de dgongs pa rnal du bzhag pa'i don 'di gsungs so// skal ldan rig pa'i rgyal sras kyis// ma
126b2(kha): lus bya ba kun byas nas// dam pa'i bla ma brten byas te// rna brgyud bdud rtsi 'thungs pa yis// 'khor ba'i re dogs kun bcad nas// phyi nang 'jug pa'i yul med
126b3(kha): pas// ma bcos byang chub sems kyi glong // snying po shar med nub pa med// thog ma tha ma med pa'i sems// ma lus thig le'i glong brda la bas// bcos pa med kyi ci bder
126b4(kha): zhog/ phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad kyi// snying po rang byung don rtogs nas// dgongs pa rnal du bzhag pa yis// rgyal ba kun gyi ngo bor gyur// 'das pa'i sangs
126b5(kha): rgyas de bzhin gshegs// rdul gyi zhing dang rab mnyam pa// rang byung rdzogs pa'i don thob nas// dgongs pa rnal du bzhag las byung // ma byon dpal ldan de bzhin gshegs//
126b6(kha): nam mkha'i mtha' dang rab mnyam pa// rdzogs chen lhan grub don rtogs nas// dgongs pa rna la du bzhag pas 'gra ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa ni// ji skad chos rnams
126b7(kha): ma lus pa// snying po gcig tu kun 'dres pas// de nyid ma bcos dgongs pa ste// rtogs nas yan par bzhag las byung // ma skyes skye ba rang log pa// rmi lam sad pa'i spyod
127a1(kha): / yul ltar// rtogs nas don 'dzin rnal 'byor pas// ma bcos bzhag pas bde bar grol// rdo rje sems dpar rang grub pa// dpag

127a3(kha): mi 'chad// rnal 'byor skal ldan grol 'dod pas// 'thungs pa tsam gyis rnam par grol// de bas srid pa'i rgya mtsho nyid// rnal 'byor thabs ldan skyes bu yis//

127a5(kha): po gcig tu gnas// de nyid rdo rje sems dpa' ste// ma lus dngos 'di thams cad kun// ma bcos rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor la// ma lus rdo rje sems dpar ni//
127a6(kha): mngon sum gzugs kyi gnas par 'gyur// nam mkha'i mtha' dang ma nyam sbyor ba'i// rdzogs chen don la gang gnas pas// dngos po gang dang gang snang yang //
127a7(kha): dgongs pa rnal du gzhag par bya'o// dpag med ye shes 'khor lo can// sangs rgyas kun gyi snying po nyid// nam mkha' lta bu dpag med pa// rang nyid de ltar gnas
127b1(kha): par bya// mtha' dbus phyogs rigs dang bral ba// ye shes rang byung bsam mi khyab// dgag bsgrub re dogs chad pa yi// bsgom du med pa'i tshul gyis gnas// rang
127b2(kha): bzhin 'bab chu ji bzhin du// ma bsgoms rang gzhag dgongs pa'i lung // ma bcos rnal du bzhag pa ni// rang dgar gnas pa'i stobs las 'grub// dbang po gang dang gang
127b3(kha): snang ba// ye shes nam mkha'i 'od du gsal// nyi 'od nam mkha'i chu rlabs ltar// ma bcos rang grol nyid la thim// dpag med nam mkha'i rang bzhin la// shar med nyi
127b4(kha): ma'i 'od kyis gang // shar ba med cing nub pa med// nam mkha'i mthar thug par du gnas// sangs rgyas kun gyi bde chen 'di// dgongs pas ma bcos rnal gzhag pa//
127b5(kha): rim par brgyud pa'i gsang ba'i gta ra// bskal par sbyangs pa'i rnal 'byor ram// dbang po tshig chod gang rung la// glong dgu rgya mtsho bcud bsdus pa'i// dbang po yan
127b6(kha): bzhag gsang ba'i thabs// dgongs pa rnal bzhag grol ba'i lam// rnal 'byor thabs kyi gsang chen 'di// skal ldan gcig gi spyod yul te// dman pa rnams kyi spyod
127b7(kha): yul min// dgongs pa rnal gzhag ye shes yin// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ dgongs pa rnal du gzhag pa'i le'u ste
128a1(kha): lnga bcu bdun pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa de la/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs rnams kyis

128a3(kha): ni ji ltar lags// phyi ma zhes ni ji ltar lags// gsang ba zhes ni gang la bgyi// de yi brda ni ji ltar lags// de yi don ni bshad du gsol// zhes zhus so/ 6/ de nas
128a4(kha): bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rjes/ 'khor gyi tshogs la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// 'das dang da ltar ma byon pa'i// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/

128a7(kha): rje byin rlabs kyis// dus gsum rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs// tshig dang yi ger mngon sprul nas// rang rgyud dag pa'i skye bo la// 'khor ba snying por dgrol ba'i phyir//
128b1(kha): rna ba rgyud 'phrul tshig dag gi rgyud// gang gi gang la gang brgyud pas// 'di ni rgyud ces bya bar brjod// chos rnams ma lus thams cad dang // bka' rgyud theg pa ma
128b2(kha): lus kyi// brjod bya don gyi snying po ni// ma bcos rdzogs pa chen po nyid// ji snyed theg pa ma lus pa'i// thabs kyis bsgrubs pa'i 'bras bu ni// ji snyed sku

129a1(kha): ste/ phyi ma 'khor ba nyid du gsungs so// snga ma sbas pa'i rang bzhin la// phyi ma gsal bar byed pa'o// 'di ni phyi ma zhes su bshad/ 6/ sangs

130a3(kha): 'dar dang rgyal ba la sogs 'byung // dngos po gang rung snang ba la// rig pa rtse gcig brtags pa'i tshe// dbang po rgyu ba rang log nas// bde ba chen po lus su smin//

132a1(kha): 'di la mtha' dang dbus med pas// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// snang srid bde chen snying po'i rgyan// ma lus kun 'dus rig pa'i

132b6(kha): dbus med pa'i rgyud// ma bcos 'od gsal don rtogs pas// mtha' bral nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor la// mtshon cha'i 'khor lo bskor ba ltar// re dogs bral ba'i
132b7(kha): pa nyid// blang dor med pa spyod pa'i rgyud// snang srid ma bcos gzhal yas su// ma bcos sku gsung thugs kyi rgyan// sku gsum rtogs pa'i don ldan pas// ma lus
133a1(kha): dkyil 'khor chen po nyid// ma lus 'di yis ston pas na// dgod med dkyil 'khor rgyan gyi rgyud// skal ldan thugs kyi rgyal sras la// snang srid
133a2(kha): dbang gi ngo bo ru// skal ldan dbang phyag rgyal pos bstan// dbang thob rgyal sras phyir mi ldog/ dbang bskur thabs kyi ru ba'i phyir// spyi blugs dbang gi rgyud ces bya// skal
133a3(kha): ldan skyes bu rnal 'byor pa// dngos don snying po la 'jug tshe// ma bcos lhag pa'i dam tshig bzhi// phog pas ma bcos dam tshig rtogs// ma lus dam tshig 'dir
133a4(kha): 'dus shing // 'byung zhing spro ba'i snying po bas// 'da' med dam tshig rgyal po'i rgyud// ma bcos thugs kyi 'phrin las la// thabs kyi gsal te bar chad med// bya btsal
133a5(kha): zhen pa'i 'phrin las min// ma btsal rig pa'i 'phrin las nyid// rtogs shing ston par byed pas na// bya bral 'phrin las rgyud ces bya// rang byung rdzogs pa chen po la//
133a6(kha): ma bcos rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor ni// sa dang lam la rim med de// rtogs pas sa rnams dus gcig mnan// mtha' med nam mkho' lta bu la// bgrod med lam
133a7(kha): mchog ston pa'i rgyud// rang byung phyogs med nam mkha' la// ma bcos ye shes shar ba'i tshe// rkyen dang sgrib pa dran rtog rnams// rgya mtsho chu dang chu bur ltar// ma lus
133b1(kha): ye shes nyid du gas la// ma lus rang byang snying po la// sgrib med gsal bar ston pas na// rang byung yang shas gas la ba'i rgyud// ta ga sha ga yi rgyan bzhin du// ji snyed
133b2(kha): che ba'i yon tan rnams// phyogs med byin rlabs rang snang bas// lhun grub 'bras bu'i rgyud ces bya// bka' brgyud kun gyi rtsa ba ni// rang byung rdzogs chen sems kyi
133b3(kha): rgyud// de dag ji snyed bstan pa kun// thams cad 'di las 'phro zhing 'dus// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ mtshan gyi
133b4(kha): rnam grangs bstan pa'i le'u ste drug cu pa'o// // de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje la/ 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// ma bcos
133b5(kha): rang byung ye shes nyid// ma lus kun gyi rang bzhin la// rim pa'i khyad par mi gnas kyang // dbang po rtsal gyi khyad par snang // dngos don rtogs dang ma rtogs pa'i//
133b6(kha): rim pa'i khyad par bdag la gsungs// zhes gsol to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa gsang ba'i bdag pos 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rang byung 'od gsal mtha' dbus
133b7(kha): med// thams cad ma bcos byang chub sems// dri med nam mkha'i glong brdal bas// rnam par dbye ba'i chos mi gnas// ma lus rang snang bstan pa ste// rig pa
134a1(kha): 'khor lor brda yis bsgrags// rang byung bstan pa thugs kyi bcud// rang bzhin khyad par 'od du 'bar// dper na nyi 'od rin chen bzhin// dbang po med
134a2(kha): pa'i yul min te// skal med rigs chad rnal 'byor pas// ji ltar btsal bar mi rnyed kyang // gang ltar bltas kyang mi mthong ngo // dmigs bral nam mkha'i yul las 'das//
134a3(kha): rang byung snying por cir mi gnas// rtogs dang ma rtogs mtha' yas kyang // snying po'i ngang la de dag med// ma lus thugs kyi bstan pa 'di// rang bzhin 'od gsal chen po nyid//
134a4(kha): ma bcis bde ba chen po'i glong // rang sems bde ba chen po'i glong // rang sems phyogs med nam mkha'i dbyings// mthar thug med pa'i ngo bor gnas// rgyal ba kun gyi don
134a5(kha): chen dbyings// mthar thug med pa'i ngo bor gnas// rgyal ba kun gyi don chen dbyings// ma bcos rin chen gter gyi gling // rin chen lhun grub snying po 'di// rin chen
134a6(kha): 'phrul gyi lde mig gis// tha mal zhen pa rnam par bzlog/ brtags pa'i 'du shes rnam par bkrol// rang snang rig pa'i 'khor lor bcug/ sgra bral bstan pa rgya mtsho
134a7(kha): gsungs// 'byed dang 'grol dang nges par 'byin// gsang ba'i lam la mngon du zhugs// re dogs gnyis 'dzin rnam par bcad// rgyu dang 'bras bu ka nas bzlog/ bcing grol
134b1(kha): med pa thar pa'i lam// phyogs med rgyas pa'i 'od snang ba// rang sems dkyil 'khor glong nas shar// rang byung thig le sems kyi ro// brda bral mnyam pa'i sems kyi myong //
134b2(kha): rig pa'i 'khor lor kun bskor bas// sgro dang skur pa rang bzhin chad// thams cad bde ba chen po'i dbyings// 'od gsal rgyu 'das rim 'jug med// dang por rtogs pa'i rang
134b3(kha): bzhin ni// rgya mtsho chu 'dzin lta bur gnas// rang gi mtshan nyid gsal rtogs pa// 'bru bcud nyams su myong ltar gnas// tha ma rin chen sbyangs pa ltar// rang byung //
134b4(kha): yon tan lhun gyis grub// rang byung rtogs shing don thob na// 'khor ba ma btsal sangs rgyas sa// bde ba chen po'i don stor ba// mtshan ma sna tshogs lam du zhugs//
134b5(kha): bya bral lhun grub snying po la// rang rang zhen pa'i mdud pas bcings// rang las 'bras bu gzhan du btsal// ri dgas smig rgyu bsnyegs pa yis// 'dod pa'i don dang
134b6(kha): gi la phrad// gang zhig nam mkha'i mtha' 'tshol ba// mi rnyed blun po'i rang bzhin ltar// sangs rgyas btsal bsgrub thob 'dod pa// mi mkhas rang bzhin de bzhin no//
134b7(kha): gang zhig skal pas dman pa la// bdud rtsi sdug bsngal rang bzhin ltar// snod min rang bzhin rigs chad la// bslab cing sdug bsngal rgyu 'gyur ba// dam pa rnams kyis/
135a1(kha): shes pa las// dman pa rnams kyis ga la shes// bcos pa'i thabs la rten nas ni// rnal ma'i lam la gzung par bya// nor bu rin chen 'od 'ang/
135a2(kha): ba// kun gyi yul du mi 'gyur bas// dam pa gsang ba'i snying po 'di// su yi snying la 'od 'bar ba// skal ldan rnal 'khyor dbang phyug ste// sku gsung thugs ni dbyings la
135a3(kha): skyong // skal med dman pa'i rnal 'byor la// brgyud pa'i thabs ni bsngags pa yin// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ gdam pa phog
135a4(kha): pa'i tshul bstan pa'i le'u ste drug cu gcig pa'o// de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa de la/ 'dus po chen po'i tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol
135a5(kha): to// dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyi// rang byung dgos pa'i bdag po khyod// gang zag blo yi khyad par ltar// bstan pa 'tsham par bstan dgos pas// slob dpon slob/
135a6(kha): ma'i khyad par dag/ ma 'dres rim par bshad du gsol// zhes gsol to// de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa des 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// dang po phyi yi bla ma
135a7(kha): yang // rim pa bzhin du brtag par bya// rang bzhin bzang dang g.yo sgyu med// drang zhing gsong por gnas pa dang / thabs chen rigs bzang 'dul ba dang // ser sna chung zhing brtse sems
135b1(kha): che// 'di ni rang bzhin brtags pa yin// gzi brjid byin rlabs che ba dang // 'gro ba 'dul dang dam chos 'du// mang po 'du zhing bsgo ba nyan// 'di ni bsod nams brtags pa yin//
135b2(kha): gang du dam pa'i rigs gyur cing // dam par gyur pa'i tshad ldan pas// 'di dag dam pa'i rang bzhin te// dam pa'i rigs kyi dam par bya// 'di ni phyi yi bla ma yin// rang bzhin de dag mi
135b3(kha): ldan cing // dam pa'i thabs la mi mkhas pas// log pa'i lha spyod dbang gyur cing // lta spyod dman pa'i lcags kyis bsdams// bdag 'dzin log pa'i ngo bor zhe na// cod 'ong
135b4(kha): lam sna sgo 'byed cing // log pa'i tshig dang thur ma yis// shes rab mig dang bral byed pas// bdag kyang bde bar nus min na// pha rol thar par ji ltar 'gyur// 'di dag rang bzhin
135b5(kha): brtag byas la// dam par 'dod pa'i gang zag gis// rmi lam du yang mi phrad na// dam par brten pa smos ci dgos// dam pa gsum gyi rim brgyud pa'i// thugs kyi gter chen rin
135b6(kha): po che// rang byung thugs kyi snang ba yis// bde chen snying po nyid 'bar ba// gsang ba'i thugs su tshud pa la// yul dang 'byung ba ma lus dang // sgo gsum dran rtog ma lus pa//
135b7(kha): ji snyed snang grags ma lus kun// bde chen rang byung mngon ston pa'i// bla ma'i zhal du snang ba yin// ma lus rang byung byang chub sems// phyogs ris med pa'i glong brdal bas//
136a1(kha): chos nyid rang bzhag rkyen gyur las// gol sgrib ga yang sa chod pa yin// snang ba sems su mthar phyin nas// sems nyid phyogs 'das bstan gyur
136a2(kha): pa/ rang sems lhun grub rin po che// mchog gi bla ma bral ba med// ji srid rol pa rang snang ba// sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya ste// re dogs bcad pa'i yon tan phyir// che
136a3(kha): ba'i yon tan chen por gnas// bla ma gnyis dang bral gyur na// phyi yi bla ma rnam pa ste// mtshan ma brda yi rjes 'brangs nas// bde chen mchog gi lam bral lo// rdo rje slob ma'i
136a4(kha): rang bzhin yang // gus dang 'dul dang snying rje che// ser sna chags pa nga rgyal chung // 'di dag rang bzhin dam pa'i rtags// dad pas dus gsum mi 'bral zhing // dam pas
136a5(kha): dam par rang mthong na// rigs dang yo byad spyod lam dag/ dman par gyur kyang dam pa yin// dam pa ma yin slob ma la// dam par bzung zhing bstan pa dang // rna ba rgyud bdud
136a6(kha): rtsi gang ston pa// gnyis ka rdo rje'i khab tu ltung // dang por dad dang gang rtogs pa'i// sgo gsum bsam pa rtse gcig pa'i// snga ma'i dran rtog rgyun bcad pa'i// rig pa 'phen
136a7(kha): pa dang po nyid// gsal bar myong phyir slob ma ste// dngos po phyi nang ma lus pa// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i cha bzung nas// rang byung ye shes chu rgyun dag/ sems nyid de la 'jug par
136b1(kha): bstan// gang zhig brda don la chags pa'i// rig pa'i gang yin slob ma ste// rang sems brda don gang bral ba// de nyid de yi gang rtogs pa// bla mas byin gyis brlabs pa mchog
136b2(kha): de ltar brda don grol gyur te// re dogs 'du shes zad gyur te// bla mar slob ma nyid grub pas// ma lus slob dpon slob ma dang // gong 'og khyad par rim med de// rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid
136b3(kha): du 'grub// ces gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ gang zag khyad par bshad pa'i le'u ste drug cu gnyis pa'o// /
136b4(kha): de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa la/ 'dus pa chen po'i tshogs rig pa rang snang gi 'khor tshogs kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sku
136b5(kha): gsung thugs kyi rang bzhin nyid// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// bstan dang bris dang bklag pa dang // gzung dang rtogs dang bsgom pa yis// yon tan nyid dam ma mos pa'i//
136b6(kha): yon tan skyon rnams bshad du gsol// zhes gsol to// de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje dam pa des 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// sangs rgyas kun gyi rin chen gter//
136b7(kha): sku gsung thugs ni mngon phyung ba// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// 'das dang ma byon da ltar gyi// sku gsung thugs ni ro gcig pa'i// ma lus gcig tu bsdus pa'i rgyud// rna
137a1(kha): brgyud rin chen 'chang ba'i mis// skal ldan rgyal chen dam pa dang // ma nor nges par bshad bstan pa// sangs rgyas dgongs pa nyid la sbyor// sangs rgyas
137a2(kha): bstan pa bshad pa yin// bstan cing bshad pas grol bar 'gyur// rin chen sna bdun la sogs la// rgyal ba kun gyi rang bzhin gyis// ma lus bsdus pa'i ngo bo nyid// sku gsung thugs
137a3(kha): nyid bris pa yin// de bas rgyal ba kun bris pa'i// che ba'i yon tan bsam mi khyab// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// rgyal ba kun gyi sku gsung thugs// rdul
137a4(kha): snyed rgyal ba ma lus pa'i// nges don ma bcos gsungs pa'i tshig/ brjod pa rgya mtsho kun gyi sgra// thos pas sgrib pa rnam 'joms shing // bklags pa nyid kyis mngon sangs rgyas//
137a5(kha): rgyal ba kun gyi gsang yin pas// bklags pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin 'di// bshad dang glegs bam ngon nyid ni// ma nor rig pa'i
137a6(kha): dkyil 'khor du// dran pas bzung ba'i don nyid ni// nam mkha'i mthar thug ji tsam par// de bas de ni lhag par 'gyur// rin chen rgyu dang dar ras dang // gro ga shing shun la sogs te//
137a7(kha): gsang ba'i rgyud 'di rab bris te// rin chen khri la legs bzhag ste// gus pas mchod cing rab bzung nas// ji srid gnas par bsam pa yi// dga' ba'i bsam pas 'dzin byed na//
137b1(kha): sangs rgyas thams cad bzung ba yin// rnam grol bla na med pa'i lam// sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs brgyud pa// ma bcos gsang ba'i don bcud 'di// gang gis rtogs pas sgro
137b2(kha): skur chad// nges pa rnyed pas dbugs 'byin phyir// 'khor ba rmi lam lta bur sangs// snying por nam mkha'i 'od ltar rgyas// dgongs pa rgya mtsho'i glong ltar brdal// 'bras bu/
137b3(kha): rin chen 'od ltar 'grub// ma bcos snying po'i don rtogs nas// rang nyams tshad dang mthun sbyar te// bar chad med par gang bsgoms pas// bsgom zhing bsgrub pa yod ma yin//
137b4(kha): ma yangs gnas pas bsgom pa ni// kun bzang rdo rje sems dpa' ste// sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin yin// ma bsgoms yengs pa med pa'i sems// ma gzhag rgyal ba'i dgongs
137b5(kha): pa'i glong // ma bcos 'od gsal brda bral sems// mtha' dbus 'dzin med dbu ma'i lam// sangs rgyas kun gyi ngo bo yin// rgyal ba kun gyi gsang ba'i gter//
137b6(kha): ma bcos snying po don gyi rgyud// rdo rje rig pa 'phrul gyi tshig/ rna brgyud thugs kyi rin chen 'di// rna ba rgyud 'phrul tshig mi ldan par// rang rtags log par zhe na dbang gis//
137b7(kha): bstan cing bshad par gyur pa dang // spel ba'ang nges par lhung 'gyur na// log pa'i don la zhen dbang gis// phyogs kyi ri bos zil mnan nas// ma bcos gsang mdzod chen po//
138a1(kha): la// skur 'debs gsang ba'i dam sri ste// ston cing smra ba'i gang zag dang // skur 'debs ma mos gang zag la// bar ma'i srid pa mi 'byung ste//
138a2(kha): rdo rje'i khab du lhung gyur te// dran pa tsam gyis skye bar 'gyur// de nas de yi tshe tsha ni// gang gis brjod par mi nus te// gal te thar par gyur pa na// gsang ba'i rna
138a3(kha): brgyud man ngag dang // bskal pa chen po brgyad khri'i bar// phrad cing mthong bar mi 'gyur te// gsang ba'i theg pas 'phongs par 'gyur// de phyir gsang ba'i bdud rtsi
138a4(kha): 'di// skal ldan rgyal sras rnal 'byor la// gsang ba'i thabs kyis gang brgyud pa// reg pas nad rnams 'tsho bar 'gyur// skal med rnams la gang bstan
138a5(kha): yang // dgra bzhin spyod dang skur pa dang // skrag cing dngang par gyur pa'i phyir// skal med dman pa'i rnal 'byor la// ming tsam bstan par mi bya zhing // glegs bam nyid
138a6(kha): ni bstan pa min// gsang chen gsang ba'i bstan pa 'di// gu lang lung gi gser gzo ru// 'jigs bral 'o ma bzhes pa ltar// skal ldan 'ga' yi spyod yul la//
138a7(kha): rigs chad las kyis dman pa yi// skal med rnams kyi spyod yul min// rin chen 'bar ba'i khong seng du// rgya ni rim pa bdun gyis btab// rigs nges skal ldan
138b1(kha): gcig la gtad// srog dang bral ba'i kha bzhin bsdams// gnas ni brag dang chu la gzhag/ ces gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las
138b2(kha): rgyud gzung ba'i le'u ste drug cu gsum pa'o// // de nas 'khor 'dus pa mang po'i tshogs kyis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje sems
138b3(kha): dpa' dang // bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje dang / gsang ba'i mdzod chen po la 'di skad ces mgrin gcig tu bstod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad
138b4(kha): kyi// rgya chen gdod nas skye ba med// nam mkha'i bdag po sna tshogs ston// sangs rgyas sku la phyag 'tshal 'dud// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ma brjod snying po
138b5(kha): don gyi gsung // gsang ba rgya mtsho ston mdzad pa// rdo rje'i gsung la bdag cag 'dud// e ma'i'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rang byung ye shes gsal ba'i thugs// ma bcos
138b6(kha): bde chen mkha' ltar gnas// bde chen thugs la phyag 'tshal 'dud// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i gter 'dzin mchog gi bdag/ ma lus gdul dka'//
138b7(kha): gsang ba'i sa la phyag 'tshal 'dud// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams da kyi// brda dang dgongs pa gsung mchog gis// ma bcos gsang ba'i don snyan pa
139a1(kha): gsang ba'i gsung la phyag 'tshal lo// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rtog bral bde chen nam mkha'i thugs// phyogs med nam mkha' rgyas pa 'dra// sangs
139a2(kha): mchog thugs la phyag 'tshal 'dud// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang mdzod bdud rtsi chen po'i glong // ma lus kun 'dus rig pa'i gter// ye shes rgya mtsho bsam mi
139a3(kha): khyab/ sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i mdzod// chos rnams ma lus thams cad kyi// snang gsal rin chen 'od kyi rgyud// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// gsang ba'i mdzod
139a4(kha): la phyag 'tshal 'dud// ces bstod do// de nas phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye
139a5(kha): ma snyed na bzhugs pa/ rdul phra mo dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kun kyang gsung gcig tu legs so legs so zhes legs par 'byin par mdzad do// sangs rgyas dang 'khor rdul snyed du
139a6(kha): bcas pa dang sa'i de bzhin nyid du grol te dgyes par gyur to// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ bstod cing yi rang ba'i le'u ste drug cu bzhi pa'o//
139a7(kha): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i dgongs pa chos thams cad nam mkha'i ngo bo/ nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam
139b1(kha): par sbyor ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud chen po rdzogs so// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po shri sing ha dang / dge slong bai ro tsa nas bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
139b2(kha): zhung tshad bam po bcu gcig pa'o// rgya gar skad du/ badz+ra satwa kha sa mAn+ta ma hA tan+t+ra/ bod skad du/ rdo rje sems dpa' nam mkha'i
139b3(kha): mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa' ye shes gsang ba la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bshad pa'i dus gcig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa yang dag par rdzogs
139b4(kha): pa'i sangs rgyas longs spyod chen po nam mkha' ltar rtag par bzhugs shing / sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje lta bur gyur pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' kun dang dbyer med pa lhun gyis
139b5(kha): grub pa'i dbang phyug/ nyi ma stong ltar brdal cing lhag pa'i che ba dang ldan pa/ thams cad gcig gi ngo bor gyur pa/ gang dang yang tha mi dad pa chen po dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas
139b6(kha): thams cad 'dus pa'i dpal rdo rje sems dpa' dang / 'og min gyi gnas chos kyi dbyings sgro skur dang bral ba/ rig pa ye shes 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang mtha' dang dbus med pa
139b7(kha): nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa/ ye shes gsang ba'i yang gsang ba/ kun tu khyab bdal chen po'i tshad dang ldan pa/ rgya dpag tu med pa/ zab cing phra la rtogs par dka' ba'i
140a1(kha): rang bzhin thug pa med cing zad 'phel med pa nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyan rab 'byams dpag tu med pas brgyan pa na/ rdzogs pa chen po bcom
140a2(kha): ldan 'das bzhugs te/ rang bzhin ngo bo'i 'khor dang / rang bzhin la rjes su lta ba'i 'khor/ rang bzhin mngon du thob pa'i 'khor la 'di lta ste/ sa dang / chu dang / me dang /
140a3(kha): rlung dang / nam mkha' dang / 'dod pa'i khams dang / gzugs kyi khams dang / gzugs med pa'i khams la sogs pa dang / yongs su rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor chen po dang /
140a4(kha): rjes su rnal 'byor dang / shin tu rnal 'byor la sogs pa thams cad dang / phyogs bcu'i 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas chos kyi sku dang

140a7(kha): gsung du gsol// zhes gsol pas/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis/ rdo rje sems dpa' chen po rdo rje la 'di skad ces gsungs so// kye ma rdo rje sems dpa'
140b1(kha): che// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// khyod ni rgyal ba kun gyi rje// rang bzhin ma bcos thugs rje yis// bya bral rdzogs lung
140b2(kha): bshad du gsol// zhes gsungs pa dang / de nas dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i chos kyi dbyings las ye shes 'phrul pa rdo rje sems dpa' zhig phyung ste/ rdo rje rtse lnga pa'i dpa
140b3(kha): bskur te 'di skad ces gsungs so// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i 'khor lo gter 'dzin cing // sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba 'chang // khyod ni
140b4(kha): smra ba'i seng ge ste// btsal med 'dul ba'i gang zag la// lhun grub theg pa gsung du gsol// zhes gsol pa dang / de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsung
140b5(kha): so// gsang sngags rdo rje nam mkha' che// tshig gi spyod yul ma yin te// brjod pas rtogs par mi 'gyur te// 'di zhes bgro bar rab tu dka'// 'on kyang dam bcas
140b6(kha): bkang ba dang // sangs rgyas thugs rje byin rlabs kyis// brda don sprad la rtogs bya'i phyir// tshig gi sgo nas spro bar bya// zhes gsungs so// de nas rdo rje sems dpa'
140b7(kha): shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mngon par dga' ba zhes bya ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pa zhes bya ba rang gi 'khor la btsal med sems nyid don rgya cher gsung
141a1(kha): ba la 'di skad ces zhus so// gzhi nyid rang byung rdo rje la// grol te 'khrul pa ji ltar 'byung // de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pas 'di skad ces
141a2(kha): gsungs so// gzhi nyid rang byung ye shes la// ma skyes pas na 'jig pa med// 'du 'bral mkha' ltar dag pa yi// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so//
141a3(kha): de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes/ dpal dang ldan pa zhes bya ba lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rin po che mngon par mtho ba la 'di skad ces gsol to// kun
141a4(kha): bzang rang byung mngon rdzogs kyis// dpag med bsam pa ji ltar bkang // zhes gsol pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par mtho bas 'di skad ces gsungs so// rang
141a5(kha): las shar ba'i don nyid las// ji ltar nyi zer nor bu ltar// ma bsags gdod nas lhun gyis rdzogs// 'gro 'ong med par kun khyab pas// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes
141a6(kha): gsungs so// de nas yang sems dpa' rdo rje des/ nub phyogs kyi 'jig rten na/ pad+ma phung po zhes bya ba na/ sangs rgyas pad+ma chags pa med pa la 'di skad ces gsol to// rang
141a7(kha): byung dag pa'i snying po la// ma rig gzung 'dzin 'khor bar 'khrul// las dang bag chags gos mi gos// de bzhin gshegs pas 'di skad ces// rang byung ye shes ka dag pas//
141b1(kha): pad+ma la ni 'dam bzhin du// mtshams med lnga yi bag chags dag/ byang chub tshul 'di bstan par bya// zhes gsungs so// de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes/ byang phyogs thams cad
141b2(kha): grub pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad grub pa la 'di skad ces gsol to// gzhi nyid lhun grub 'phrin las la// phyi nang snang srid ji ltar mdzad//
141b3(kha): ces gsungs so// de bzhin gshegs pa des 'di skad ces gsungs so// btsal med lhun grub byin rlabs las// mdzad pa'i byin rlabs phyogs bcur brda la// phyogs mi
141b4(kha): mnga' yongs kyi gter// byang chub tshul 'di bstan par bya// zhes gsungs so// de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad la 'di skad
141b5(kha): ces gsol te/ sems nyid rin chen 'phrul gyi sgo// rtogs par 'dod pas ji ltar blta// zhes gsol pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyis 'di skad ces
141b6(kha): gsungs so// 'phrul gyi skyes bu'i tshul bzhin du// gcig rtogs kun kyang de 'dra ba// ma bcos byang chub snying po la// phyogs su bltas pas mthong mi 'gyur// zhes gsungs
141b7(kha): so// de nas 'dod khams tha ma ru// ming gsum ldan pa'i skyes bu la// ltas gsum ldan phyir bskul ba'i mthus// thugs rje sems dpa'i byin rlabs kyis// 'od lnga ldan
142a1(kha): pas sku bstan te// chos kyi 'khor lo gdan stengs su// rin chen 'bar ba'i gsal bkab nas// rdo rje sems dpa' ma brjod gsungs// de nas skyes
142a2(kha): bu rgyal sras des// rig pa'i gdeng gis don rtogs nas// de tshe de yi dus nyid du// dus mtha'i skad cig nyid la ni// glong dgu bam po nyi khri nyid// skal ldan lha gnas grags
142a3(kha): par gyur// de nas thugs rje'i byin rlabs kyis// d+ha na ko sha'i gling gi phug/ lha mo sems dga' 'od zer can// sprul pa'i 'dab chags phra men 'dus// byin rlabs ye
142a4(kha): shes thugs mtshan las// ye mtshan sprul pa'i cha 'dzin cing // stong nyid btsal med sgrogs 'gyur nas// yang sbrul skal ldan sras bdun las// rgyal thabs
142a5(kha): spyi blugs dbang bskur nas// thogs med byang chub sems dang spyad// gsang ba'i 'khor lo rog pa'i gter// brda phrad tshogs med don po che// ma btsal rang dgar bzhag
142a6(kha): pos 'grub// dpog tu med pa'i rgyal ba yis// phun sum tshogs pa kun 'dus nas// bstan pa bsam las gsungs pa yang // grong dgu'i nang du ma 'dus med/
142a7(kha): skal ldan thugs rje shes pa yis// dus gcig nyid la rtogs pa'i lus// rdo rje nam mkha' kyil po che// mtha' dbus sprod pa rnam par bcad// blon mi mi shes
142b1(kha): 'khor lo can// bskur med rang gas la brjod dang bra la// dgongs pa nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam// mtshan ma'i spros pa gdod nas dag/ rig pa rang snang 'khor lo la// bsam
142b2(kha): brjod sprod pa'i thabs la mkhas// ma nyam nyid rig pa'i 'khor lo la// mtshan ma sgra yi sa gtan la phab// ye shes rang byung 'khor lo las// cho 'phrul thugs rje rang bzhin
142b3(kha): 'char// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// rang byung gsang ba'i 'khor lo las// glong dgu'i bstan pa char bzhin 'byung // rang 'byung rang gsal gtan la 'bebs// rang

142b7(kha): pa'i bdag/ a ti gsum gyi ngo bo la// brda don sprad pa'i gtan tshigs kyis// bshad pa gsum la nges dgongs nas// gzhi lam 'bras bu gsungs du gsol// zhes zhus

143a3(kha): gces// rang bzhin thabs dang 'bras bu nyid// rdzogs chen ma bcos dgongs pa la// mi 'gal brjod pa'i sgra yis mtshon// dngos pa'i don nyid gtan la phab//

144a7(kha): glong du bshad// rdzogs sku mdzes khyab kun gsal bas// nyi ma 'bum bdal lta bur bshad// 'byung 'jug mi mnga' kun gnas pas// sprul sku nyi mi'i zer ltar bshad//

148a5(kha): phyung don 'di la// slob tshul rim pa ngos bzung nas// rgyal thabs spyi blugs dbang bskur bas// sems nyid rin chen rtogs bya'i phyir// de phyir lta bas thag bcad bshad//
148a6(kha): de nyid ma yengs goms bya'i phyir// brda don bral ba'i man ngag bshad// ci spyad stong 'gyur 'ching med pas// glang chen chur zhugs man ngag bshad// glong dgur 'dus pa'i
148a7(kha): tshig don spyi// rgyud kun gtan la dbab pa'i tshig/ 'dis ni bshad par bya ba yin// glong dgu lde mig phye ba yis// nyid la 'chad cing nyid kyis 'brel// btsal med theg chen
148b1(kha): gang zag la// tshig bral rig pa'i 'khor lo bskor// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las// bshad pa'i lde mig gis klong dgu dbye ba'i le'u ste
148b2(kha): gsum pa'o// // de nas sems dpa' rdo rjes/ rdo rje sems dpa' chen po la 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sku
148b3(kha): gsung thugs kyi gter 'chang ba// ye shes mdzod ldan gnyis med rdzogs// rang grol thams cad gnyis med dang // mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// ngo bo thabs kyi mtshan nyid
148b4(kha): de/ rnam grol rig pa'i gter khang dag/ mgon pos bdag la bshad du gsol// zhes gsol to// de nas de bzhin gshags pa rdo rje sems dpas bka' stsal to// kye sem
148b5(kha): dpa' chen po/ mkha' mnyam byang chub sems kyi lung // nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// rin chen dbyig dang sprad pa'i thabs// ye shes gsang rdzogs chos
148b6(kha): dbyings nyid// ngo bo gcig la brtags pas gsum// dngos dang bsam pas phye ba'i tshul// ngo bo skyon thabs mtshon pa'i dpe// bcings grol tshul gyis phye ba yin//
148b7(kha): kun 'dus nam mkha'i mtha' ma nyam la// kun tu rang gsal dbyings la rdzogs// mi gnas mi bsam cir mi dgongs// spros bral rig pa'i 'khor lo ga ti ra// sangs rgyas ma
149a1(kha): yin sems can min// gnyis ka ma yin rang shar lung // sgro dang skur pa rnam par bcad// mtha' dbus bral ba'i snying po 'di// phyogs bral rig pa'i

149a4(kha): ma gsungs rang 'byal rig pa'i sgra// bsam med rang 'byung rang gsal la// gsal la log rtog mdud pas bcings// de nyid dbyings su mi gsal na// bkrol yang thar par mi

149a7(kha): thams byo pa 'ini dang // rgyal thabs kyi thugs dbang bathur dang / theg pa'i bye brag 'byed la 'artson// brjod mams chi gdan 'brel par ston// ba don ston pa'i slo pon na/

149b2(kha): nges par gsungs// rang rig gsal bas rang la ston// rang gsal lung la rang gis mtshan// rang rig gzer chen rang la 'debs// slob du pon kun gyi mchog tu gsungs//
149b3(kha): nges pa'i seng ge'i rjes byung bas// rtsal med seng ge'i sgra sgrogs pa// dpal ldan kun mkhyen rnam grol thugs// 'jig rten gsal ba'i nyi ma bzhin// rang 'byung shes

150a1(kha): ni rnam par rtog pa ste// gcig ni ye shes gsang ba yin// dus tshod bla ma'i thugs la brtag/ rgyud pa thabs kyi me long gis// mngon du/

150a4(kha): dbus bral ba'i snying po ni// rdzogs pa thug phrad yin par gsungs// ci la snang ba'i dus de nas// ma btsal rig snang mi rtog lung // ma nyam brjod kun bral ye shes
150a5(kha): te/ bu mo dga' ba'i ro bzhin no// ye shes nyams rdzogs chag cig la// sku gsung thugs phrad man ngag gsal// kun kyang ye shes rang gsal te// dus tshod bla ma'i
150a6(kha): zhal las shes// thabs sbyor man ngag bcu gsum po// gang la 'dul ba'i thabs su bstan// so so rang rig nges bstan pa// mkhyen ldan bla ma'i zha la las shes//
150a7(kha): thabs kyi rim pa gang dang gang // ji ltar yin pa de ltar 'jug/ 'dod 'byung rin chen 'phrul gyi dbyig/ btsal med gnas pas thob par 'gyur// ngo bo gsal la dmigs

151a4(kha): gang ltar gzhag pa de ltar dbyings// rang gsal nyi ma kun la snyoms// mtha' bral nyi ma'i snying po ltar// gsal la brtags na dmigs dang bral// mi g.yo 'dzin bral mnyam

151b3(kha): rig pa'i gter la smra ba// thig le yongs kyis zlum po la// 'khor dang mya ngan ye nas med// 'khor ba byang chub snying po la// sdug bsngal kun bzang rol par shar/

151b5(kha): lngar gsal bas// ye shes nyi ltar kun la ga la// 'dod lnga yul lnga kun gyi gsos// rang 'byung thugs rje kun gyi gsoso// rang rig rol pa rang la snang // rang rig

151b7(kha): gdod nas ye shes rang gsal la// gnyis su brtags pas 'khrul pa'i lame// sku dang gsung thugs 'phrin las kun// rig pa gsal ba'i dbyings la gsal// mkha'
152a1(kha): la bya lam 'dra ba yis// nam mkha' dbyings thim gsal mi 'gyur// zhing khams dbang stobs rdzu 'phrul yang // ma nyam nyid rig pa'i gter la rdzogs//

152b4(kha): ma bcos dbyings las gzhan ma yin// nga rgyal mngon mthong lhar gsal nas// longs spyod bde sdug so so yang // ma bcos dang la gnyis med pas// gnyis med

156a1(kha): mkha'i stong pa la// rgyal bral mnyam pa'i yid kyis 'juH/ mthong med rig pa la la la gyur// yig med pa'i don du mthong / mtshan ma
156a2(kha): yi rjes 'brangs nas// spros bral rig pa'i don dang 'gal// ma btsal rang ra'abyung 'od gsal bas// mtha' dbus med pa'i dbyings la thim// gsang dang gsang chen rab
156a3(kha): gsang ba// rang gsang spros bcad gcig la 'dus// ye shes rang gsal rig pa'i 'od// phyogs ris mi mnga' yongs la snyoms// mnyam nyid rig pa'i ngo bo nyid//
156a4(kha): gang yang yin no rnam kun pas// rang rig 'pho 'gyur med pa la// ji ltar gsal yang 'di zhes med// kun gsal me long 'od po che// ye shes rdzogs pa'i ngo bo la//
156a5(kha): ya nas thig le chen po la// bdag gzhan ye shes dbyings su rdzogs// rgyal po kun gyi dbang po ltar// bla ma dam pa rdo rje ni// rdo rje sems dpa' mngon 'byung ba/
156a6(kha): 'phrul tshig rig pa'i sgron ma yin// gter khyim dpal be'u sgo phye nas// skye ba med pa'i brda don sprad// bgrod pa med par sa la gzhag/ 'chi ba med pa'i chos skur ston//
156a7(kha): rtogs pa'i shes rab glo dkar du// rang gsal nyi mas khyab par gad la// rin chen par bu'i sgo phye nas// rdo rje sems dpa'i thugs bcud bgros// thabs sbyor
156b1(kha): rig pa'i sgo bkros te// ye shes gsang ba'i man ngag bstan// sgra tshig med pa'i rog pa yis// rang gsal nyi ma'i 'od la gzhug/ rtsol sgrub bral ba'i 'bras bu smad/
156b2(kha): 'di ltar ston pa'i slob dpon ni// lus srog dbang po sha rus khrag/ bskal par btang yang mi 'phangs na// bu dang chung ma nor gyi dbyig/ bran pho bran mo smos te/
156b3(kha): dgos/ dam pa rgyal bar mi 'dzin na// dpag med rgyud la mkhas gyur kyang // de nyid gshed 'gyur snying bral na// nges par rdo rje khab tu lhung // 'gyogs 'gro so
156b4(kha): mtshams 'da' ba 'dra// 'khor ba ga ting du lhung 'gyur nas// dam pa de la ma brten par// thar pa'i skabs ni mi srid do// rdzogs chen rna ba rgyud man ngag la// bla ma'i
156b5(kha): man ngag mi ldan par// log rtog shes par spyod pa ni// nges par ltung 'gyur the tsom med// rang bzhin ngan pa'i mi rnams la// thos chung sgra la goms med dang //
156b6(kha): theg pa dman pa'i skye bo dang // rdo rje slob dpon smod pa dang // rdo rje spun la 'khu ba dang // rang gsal don la skur pa dang // khe grag che ba'i rgyu ba slu ba dang // chos la dgag sgrub
156b7(kha): byed pa dang // don med sgra la gnyer ba dang // don med slob dpon dbang 'dod la// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// yang gsang thugs kyi man ngag 'di//
157a1(kha): sabya// bshad kyang nges par ba shad byas na// dam shod gling gi dur khrod du// Da ma ru la 'du ba ltar// mkha' 'gro rna nyan 'dus pa yin// 'chi
157a2(kha): pa'i dus med sngon rol du// sha khrag mngon du zos pa dang // mi bzad drag po sdug bsngal gyis// 'chi dang nges par srog bcad nas// rdo rje khab tu nges par 'gro// byang
157a3(kha): chub sems dang ma ldan na// thar par mi 'gyur skyabs dang bral// de phyir nges pa'i dbang thob pa'i// rgyal sras nges pa gcig la gtad// ces gsungs so// nam
157a4(kha): mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/ rig pa gsal byed dpa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas sems dpa' rdo rje des/ rdo rje
157a5(kha): sems dpa' chen po la 'di skad ces gsol to// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// ye shes chen po rang shar bdag/ 'phrul tshig sgra yis mtshon pa'i phyir//
157a6(kha): brjod bral rig pa'i ngo bo la// sngon byas gdam ngag rim pa yis// gsal bar nges par gsung du gsol// zhes zhus so// de nas rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos 'di skad
157a7(kha): ces gsungs so// kye sems dpa' chen po/ nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud// rdzogs chen thugs kyi glong gi bcud// dmigs dang thabs gsol gnang ba
157b1(kha): 'di/ skyon yon rim pas brtag pa gces// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi gter 'chang zhing // rang rig gsal ba'i mi g.yo thugs// ma bcos 'od gsal 'od la
157b2(kha): bzhugs// mi gnas rtog bral rtsi'i mi dgongs// bsam bral spyod med don mnga' zhing // rig pa ma bcos dbyings la 'jug/ bsam med rig pa'i gdeng gis gnas// /
157b3(kha): bsam med spyad med sa la ba// dmigs med don la rtag tu bzhugs// rgyal thabs tshangs pa'i man ngag gis// 'khor ba ma bcos gnas su spar// gtad 'dzin
157b4(kha): bral ba'i blo yis ni// rnam rtog ye shes snying por mkhyen// sgrib pa gsal ba'i ye shes la// bcos med rig pa'i blo yis 'jug/ snying rje thabs mkhas spyod pa yis//
157b5(kha): ma lus ma bcos rig par gas la// gang dang gang gis thabs nyid kyis// bsam pa de de rims sbyar nas// mos 'jug tha dad dbang gis na// dus gcig 'gro ba
157b6(kha): byang chu pa las// spros bral rig pa'i dkyil 'khor la// bcos med rig pa'i sems kyi gnas// byar med lhun grub 'a phrin las la// bya ba tshul med
157b7(kha): par rang bzhin gnas// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid la// ma bgrod lam kun rdzogs par gas la// 'phrul tshig rig pa'i sgron ma yis// bsam pa'i
158a1(kha): b+he brag ji bzhin gsal// dbang dang byin rlabs thabs ldan zhing // rdo rje mchog gi rnal 'byor ro// yon tan bcud 'dzin rdo rjeg
158a2(kha): dam par gnas pa'i gang zag gis// g.yo sgyu ma dang sems bral zhing // 'bab chu dge slong tshul 'dzin pa// sgo gsum dran pa'i sgo nyid nas// lus dang ngag
158a3(kha): sems yo byad dang // zhing dang bran pho bran mo dang // chung ma ga ser dngul rin chen lnga// bu dang bu mo rkang 'gros 'bru// 'phangs med bsam pas gtang bar bya
158a4(kha): de nas spyod dang bsnun pa dang // ba yu lde dang nyams bskyed dang // yun rings dam pa mi gdags pas// grags pa gsol dang bsnyung bar bzhag/ gang nis de la dbo ba
158a5(kha): da / las len spyod par bawA pa dang // bkru dang phyug bag ma rlung 'bru dang // slos dab rgyad gsod man 'dor dang // thams cad bka' migacig pams// dam
158a6(kha): bco brgyad spyad byas nas// mgon porang gsal thums mang 'a zhing // rang gsal 'od la ma nyam drug nas// spos mang du yis gats+tshag tu// rdzogs chen rang rigags
158a7(kha): la 'dun/ khyod kyi ye shes snying po la// rang rig gis ni mtshon pa'i phyir// ma brjod rig pa'i gsung gis ni/ bdag la rig pa'i don gsam mdzod// rangs
158b1(kha): gsal nges rtogs pa'i// ma bcos rig pa'i bu khyod la// btsal med rig pa nges bstan gyis// blo yi ga ting du go bar byos// gal te dam tshig 'das pa la// gsang ba'i
158b2(kha): ye shes bshad dam brjod// rdzogs chen rna brgyud 'di bstan na// bul ba ri yi 'bru bzhin du// de ma thag tu brlag pa dang // mkha' 'gro dam can 'dus 'gyur nas//
158b3(kha): dur khrod 'bar ba'i ro gling du// gcan gzan 'dus nas btod bzhin 'gyur// rdo rje bla ma long ba nyid// nges par yang yin gnas su 'gro// de la brten cing lam ltos
158b4(kha): pa// smos ci dgos te rig dang bral// rig dang ldan des sngon 'gros sbyangs// yon tan kun tshang bu mchog la// dbang bskur byin rlabs nyams byin nas// nyi ma stong
158b5(kha): gi 'od ltar 'gyur// kun gyi dbang bskur gnas thob nas// ye shes rang gsal 'od la zhugs// bde ba phrag brgya'i ro myong nas// de nyid tsam gyis rdzogs sangs rgyas//
158b6(kha): btsal med gnas pa'i rnal 'byor la// lung du zhugs pa'i rig pa yis// bcos med 'od gsal nyid du shar// nam mkha'i mtha' dang ma nyam sbyor bas// yon tan
158b7(kha): grangs med snying por rdzogs// de ltar bla ma mnyes byas nas// rin chen dpal be'u'i sgo phye nas// gang ltar yin pa'i thabs yin gyis// rin tshon ngo sa bstan drod tshad
159a1(kha): bshad/ rgyud pa thabs kyi me long gis// mngon gsal rin chen 'bar ba la// mtshon cing rtag pa ma yin yang // 'dul dbang ngo la de ltar gsal/
159a2(kha): thig le 'od gsal ting 'dzin gyis// tha dad mi gas la gcig la gnas// gnas med rang gsal ye shes pas// 'bab chu 'dra ba'i man ngag sbyong // mi gnas drag po'i
159a3(kha): glong nyid la// glang chen stod pa'i man ngag sbyin// 'dir yang mi gnas 'gro ba la// glang chen phyal pa sbyin par bya// 'dzin med ya la ba'i gang zag la// gzugs ldan rig
159a4(kha): pa'i man ngag sbyin// thabs dang shes rab rtag 'chang bas// kha sbyar ba ru'i man ngag sbyin// skal med dbang po dman pa la// shin tu gdams pa'i man ngag sbyin// phyi nang
159a5(kha): gsang ba'i gang zag la// bgrang dang gzung dang brtag pa dang // thung mong rlung gi man ngag sbyin// blo ldan rtogs pa'i gang zag la// 'phrul gyi me long man ngag sbyin//
159a6(kha): chags zhen 'dod pa'i rig can la// rin chen bde skyil man ngag sbyin// rtag 'dzin de nyid rig can la// ngo bo rtag pa'i man ngag sbyin// shes ldan dbang po dul ba
159a7(kha): la/ brda ldan rig pa'i man ngag sbyin// yul la zhen pa'i gang zag la// dbang po brtul ba'i thabs kyis bstan// tshig la dga' ba'i gang zag la// sgra la brtag
159b1(kha): pa'i man ngag sbyin// rgyun du ma nyam gzhog 'dri ba la// spyod lam rgyun gyi man ngag phog/ blo ldan skal ldan yang ra ba la// chu bsres lta bu'i man ngag sbyin// 'dzun
159b2(kha): rtsol bral ba'i rig pa la// 'jug med rig pa de ltar lta// 'od gsal ma bcos dang du gzhag/ rjes mi 'brang zhing yul mi 'tsho la// rang gsal skyon bral cis
159b3(kha): mi 'khrug/ rang la mi bsam dbyings mi 'tshol// 'dod shes kun bral gsal ba'i 'od// phyogs bral kun khyab dmigs su med// de dogs bsam spyad
159b4(kha): mtha' las grol// phyogs bral nyi 'od 'bar bltar// byin rlabs yongs su khyab par brda la// nor bu rin chen 'bar ba ltar// kun la de ltar nyid du ston//
159b5(kha): btsa la bral rig pa'i rang gsal la// 'byung 'jug 'dzin pa kun dang bral// zhes gsungs so// nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud chen po las/

160a3(kha): rang rig ye shes dkyil 'khor la// rnag pa'i tha skad kun dang bral// phyogs bral mnyam pa'i dkyil 'khor las// gang sbyar bsdus pa de ltar gas so//

160a5(kha): gtsug gi rang bzhin la// mtshan ma'i tha snyad kun dang bral// rang gsal thabs kyi me long la// 'gag myed kun gyi gzugs brnyan 'char// de nyid ma bcod
160a6(kha): rang gsal zlum// sgro bral rig pa'i gdung la gnas// ma bcos rang gsal mkha' ltar dag/ mi gnas nam mkha' lta bu'i tshul// gdod nas dag pa'i

164a1(kha): gsang ba'i don ma rtogs// rgyal thabs rig pa'i dbang ma thob// gnyis med rang gsal nyag gcig la// nges med gnyis kyi cha 'dzin gyis//
164a2(kha): 'dod la nges pa'i 'bras bu gcig/ 'dod pa 'khrul pa rig can de// gnyis kyi gnyis med ji ltar nyid// 'ching bus gser bu ma mi gcig dang // nges pa med pas khe bor
